#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0001 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x0002 [0x03] Work_Zone[1] = 1*
  2: 0x0007 [0x43] SEND_EVENT_UPDATE: Send pending tag to server (packet 0x005B)
  3: 0x0009 [0x43] SEND_EVENT_UPDATE: Check pending flag (skip if not pending)
  4: 0x000B [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1] = Work_Zone[3]
  5: 0x0010 [0x5D] SET_MUSIC_VOLUME(volume=0*, fade_time=120*)
  6: 0x0015 [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x3342)
  7: 0x0018 [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Disable user control
  8: 0x001A [0x38] SET_CLIENT_EVENT_MODE(mode=27*)
  9: 0x001D [0x2F] Volto Oscuro (ID: 16924803/0x01024083)->Render.Flags0 &= ~0x80000 // Bit 19
 10: 0x0023 [0x2F] Unnamed NPC (ID: 16924804/0x01024084)->Render.Flags0 &= ~0x80000 // Bit 19
```
